<h1 _ngcontent-pss-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="arEngine（AR增强现实能力）"> arEngine（AR增强现实能力） </h1>

<div _ngcontent-pss-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>本模块提供AR Engine（AR引擎服务）的arEngine（AR增强现实能力）相关接口。</p>    <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AREngine.Core</p>    <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.1.0(18)</p>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="section13899175210107" device-type="phone,tablet">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section13899175210107" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><div _ngcontent-pss-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-pss-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-pss-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-pss-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-pss-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-pss-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-pss-c106="" class="handle-button id="section913918490464" device-type="phone,tablet">ARAddAugmentedImageMode<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section913918490464" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>枚举，添加图片模式。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AREngine.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.1.0(18)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.5.1.4.1.1" width="30%">          <p><strong>名称</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.5.1.4.1.2" width="20%">          <p><strong>值</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.5.1.4.1.3" width="50%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>NORMAL</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>0</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>正常模式。</p>          <p>当添加的图片数量超过默认的最多图片数量（50）时，AR Engine会报告错误，错误信息见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arengine-error-code#section4676153191213">1009200011</a>。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>UPDATE</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>1</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>更新模式。</p>          <p>当添加的图片数量超过默认的最多图片数量（50）时，AR Engine会删除原有的最旧数据，以添加新的图片。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1589px;">     <h2 id="section7453144131020" device-type="phone,tablet">ARAddAugmentedImageReason<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section7453144131020" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>枚举，添加图像失败原因。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AREngine.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.1.0(18)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.5.1.4.1.1" width="30%">          <p><strong>名称</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.5.1.4.1.2" width="20%">          <p><strong>值</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.5.1.4.1.3" width="50%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>NONE</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>0</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>无失败原因，图像成功添加。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>SIZE_NOT_MATCH</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>1</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>图像尺寸不正确。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002329946638__p18444125201619">图像尺寸评价从宽高比、分辨率两个维度进行。建议宽高比、分辨率的评价为Unfit以上。</p>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>LIGHT_ANOMALY</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>2</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>图像亮度过亮或过暗。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>FEATURE_LIMIT</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>3</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>图像颜色单一，如纯色图片。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>OTHER</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>4</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>其他原因，如图片有反光、光斑，重复性内容等。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <ul id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002329946638__ul6624184216143">      <li id="li4624174221415">宽高比：       <div class="p" id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002329946638__p19553974510">        图像宽度与高度之比，如：640*480分辨率的图像，其宽高比为1.33，对应评价Excellent。         <div class="tablenoborder">         <div class="tbBox"><table id="table1181224184010"  <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">             <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002329946638__p174113462404">[6, ∞)</p></td>            <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">             <p        <p id="ZH-CN_TOPIC_0000002329946638__p1141104644014">[4, 6)</p></td>            <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">             <p <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AREngine.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.1.0(18)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.5.1.4.1.1" width="30%">          <p><strong>名称</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.5.1.4.1.2" width="20%">          <p>1</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>开启深度模式。</p>          <p>AR Engine会自动尝试从多种深度源获取深度信息。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <p>通常有两种深度源，运动算法和硬件深度传感器 (Time of Flight，简称ToF)。</p>            <p>目前仅支持运动算法。</p>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AREngine.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.1.0(18)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.5.1.4.1.1" width="30%">          <p><strong>名称</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.5.1.4.1.2" class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 497px;">     <h2 id="section4381141123516" device-type="phone,tablet">Distortion<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section4381141123516" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>type Distortion = [number, number, number, number, number]</p>     <p>类型别名，用于表示一个包含五个数字的数组，为相机的畸变系数。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AREngine.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.1.0(18)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">    <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="67.64%">          <p>表示值类型为数字，相机内参，取值范围无限制。</p>          <p>其中Distortion [0]~Distortion [2]表示k1，k2，k3（径向畸变系数），Distortion [3]~Distortion [4]是切向畸变系数。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 326px;">     <h2 id="section1410345414514" Promise&lt;ARAddAugmentedImageResult&gt;</p>     <p>将图像添加到图像数据库，并输出对应图像的索引。</p>     <p>使用Promise异步回调返回ARAddAugmentedImageResult对象。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AREngine.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本</strong><strong>：</strong>5.1.0(18)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1116px;">     <h3 id="section14343257201916" device-type="phone,tablet">ARSession.detachAnchor<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arengine-api-arengine#section63641154194411">ARAnchor.release</a>来释放锚点。</p>      </div></div></div> arEngine.<span class="hljs-property">ARSceneMesh</span> = frame.<span class="hljs-title function_">acquireSceneMesh</span>();</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1037px;">     <h3 id="section8978424152512" device-type="phone,tablet">ARFrame.acquireDepthImage16Bits<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section8978424152512" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>acquireDepthImage16Bits(): ARImage</p>     <p>获取当前帧对应的深度图像对象。</p>     <p>深度图像是索引0处的单个16位平面。每个像素包含到相机平面的距离，以mm为单位，可表示的深度范围在0mm~65535mm之间，即约65m。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AREngine.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.1.0(18)</p>     <div class="p">      <strong>返回值：</strong>      <div class="tablenoborder">       <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.65.7.2.1.3.1.2" width="70%">           <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>         </tr><tr>          <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">           <p><a </tr>               </tbody></table></div>      </div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>acquireDepthConfidenceImage(): ARImage</p>     <p>获取当前帧的深度置信度图像。</p>     <p>置信度值为0、1和2，0表示估计深度值的置信度最低，1表示估计深度值置信度中等，2表示估计深度值置信度最高，深度置信度图像的宽高与深度图像一致。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AREngine.Core</p> id="mcps1.3.69.6.1.6.1.2" width="28.33%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.69.6.1.6.1.3" width="10.190000000000001%">          <p>只读</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.69.6.1.6.1.4" width="10.4%">          <p>可选</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.69.6.1.6.1.5" width="27.96%"> <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="27.96%">          <p>从相机到命中位置的距离，单位为m，其值范围0~65535。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1165px;">     <h3 id="section1864219177109" device-type="phone,tablet" class="firsth2">ARHitResult.getHitPose<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1864219177109" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span></div><p>getHitPose(): ARPose</p>     <p>获取交点位姿。</p>     <p>位姿信息可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arengine-coordinate" target="_blank">坐标系说明</a>。</p>     <p>如果<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arengine-api-arengine#section188141239153515">ARPointOrientationMode</a>是ESTIMATED_SURFACE_NORMAL，则 X+ 是射线的垂直向量，也就是平面的平行向量，Y+ 是平面的法向量，Z+ 是平面的平行向量，大致指向相机。</p>     <p>如果<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arengine-api-arengine#section188141239153515">ARPointOrientationMode</a>是INITIALIZED_TO_IDENTITY，则坐标的旋转不会随着平面的角度变化而变化。X+ 是射线的垂直向量，指向右侧（从设备的视角），Y+ 指向上方，Z+ 大致指向相机。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AREngine.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.1.0(18)</p>     <div class="p">      <strong>返回值：</strong> <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>         </tr><tr>          <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">           <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arengine-api-arengine#section19274193834913">ARPose</a>对象并返回。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.AREngine.Core</p> width="27.122712271227122%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.102.7.1.5.1.3" width="18.631863186318633%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th    </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="27.122712271227122%">          <p>translation</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="27.122712271227122%">          <p><a
